            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                Category <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              <select
                name="RFQCategory"
                value={form.RFQCategory}
                onChange={handleChange}
                required
              >
                <option value="">-- Select --</option>
                {rfqCategories.map((c, i) => (
                  <option key={i} value={c}>
                    {c}
                  </option>
                ))}
              </select>
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                RFQ Reference <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              <textarea
                name="RFQreference"
                value={form.RFQreference}
                onChange={handleChange}
                rows={4}
                cols={40}
                maxLength={250}
                placeholder="Enter RFQ Reference..."
                required
              />
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>Register Dt. Comments</label>
              <textarea
                name="Comments"
                value={form.Comments}
                onChange={handleChange}
                rows={4}
                cols={40}
                maxLength={250}
                placeholder="Your Comments Here..."
              />
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
        {/* end enq-main-grid */}

        <hr className="enq-divider" />

        <div className="enq-bottom-grid">
          {/* ── QUOTE SECTION ───────────────────────────────────────── */}
          <div className="enq-section">
            <div className="enq-section-title">Quote</div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>Quote Number</label>
              <p className="enq-readonly enq-qn">{form.Quotenumber}</p>
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>Register Date</label>
              <input
                type="date"
                name="RFQREGDate"
                value={form.RFQREGDate}
                readOnly
              />
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>Stage</label>
              <select
                name="Quotestage"
                value={form.Quotestage}
                onChange={handleChange}
              >
                <option value="">-- Select Stage --</option>
                {quoteStages.map((s, i) => (
                  <option key={i} value={s}>
                    {s}
                  </option>
                ))}
              </select>
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>Quote Submitted Date</label>
              <input
                type="date"
                name="Quotesubmitteddate"
                value={form.Quotesubmitteddate}
                onChange={handleChange}
              />
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                Opportunity Stage <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              <select
                name="Opportunitystage"
                value={form.Opportunitystage}
                onChange={handleChange}
                required
              >
                <option value="">-- Select --</option>
                {oppStages.map((s, i) => (
                  <option key={i} value={s}>
                    {s}
                  </option>
                ))}
              </select>
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>Revision</label>
              <p className="enq-readonly">0</p>
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                Expected Order Date <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              <input
                type="date"
                name="Expectedorderdate"
                value={form.Expectedorderdate}
                onChange={handleChange}
                required
              />
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row enq-row-inline">
              <div>
                <label>Effective Enquiry Date</label>
                <input
                  type="date"
                  name="EffEnqDate"
                  value={form.EffEnqDate}
                  onChange={handleChange}
                  disabled={!form.enableEffEnqDate}
                  className={!form.enableEffEnqDate ? "enq-disabled-field" : ""}
                />
              </div>
              <input
                type="checkbox"
                name="enableEffEnqDate"
                checked={form.enableEffEnqDate}
                onChange={handleChange}
                title="Enable Effective Enquiry Date"
              />
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>Priority</label>
              <select
                name="Priority"
                value={form.Priority}
                onChange={handleChange}
              >
                <option value="Low">Low</option>
                <option value="Medium">Medium</option>
                <option value="High">High</option>
              </select>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* ── PRODUCT SECTION ─────────────────────────────────────── */}
          <div className="enq-section">
            <div className="enq-section-title">Product</div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                Facing Factory <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              {form.isCustomFacingfactory ? (
                <div className="enq-custom-row">
                  <input
                    type="text"
                    name="FacingfactoryCustom"
                    value={form.FacingfactoryCustom}
                    onChange={handleChange}
                    maxLength={25}
                    placeholder="Enter Facing Factory..."
                  />
                  <input
                    type="checkbox"
                    checked={form.isCustomFacingfactory}
                    onChange={(e) => {
                      setForm((prev) => ({
                        ...prev,
                        isCustomFacingfactory: e.target.checked,
                      }));
                    }}
                  />
                </div>
              ) : (
                <div className="enq-custom-row">
                  <select
                    name="Facingfactory"
                    value={form.Facingfactory}
                    onChange={(e) => handleFacingFactoryChange(e.target.value)}
                  >
                    <option value="">-- Select --</option>
                    {facingFactories.map((f, i) => (
                      <option key={i} value={f}>
                        {f}
                      </option>
                    ))}
                  </select>
                  <input
                    type="checkbox"
                    checked={form.isCustomFacingfactory}
                    onChange={(e) => {
                      setForm((prev) => ({
                        ...prev,
                        isCustomFacingfactory: e.target.checked,
                      }));
                    }}
                  />
                </div>
              )}
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                Product <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              <select
                name="Product"
                value={form.Product}
                onChange={handleProductChange}
                multiple
                required
              >
                <option value="" disabled>
                  Select a product
                </option>
                {products.map((p, i) => (
                  <option key={i} value={p}>
                    {p}
                  </option>
                ))}
              </select>
              <small className="enq-hint">
                Hold Ctrl / Cmd to select multiple
              </small>
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                Project Name <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              <textarea
                name="Projectname"
                value={form.Projectname}
                onChange={handleChange}
                rows={4}
                cols={40}
                maxLength={75}
                placeholder="Enter Project Name..."
                required
              />
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                Customer Due Date <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              <input
                type="date"
                name="CustomerdueDate"
                value={form.CustomerdueDate}
                onChange={handleChange}
                required
              />
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>Proposed Due Date</label>
              <input
                type="date"
                name="ProposeddueDate"
                value={form.ProposeddueDate}
                onChange={handleChange}
              />
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                Lines in RFQ <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              <input
                type="number"
                name="Totallineitems"
                value={form.Totallineitems}
                onChange={handleChange}
                maxLength={4}
                placeholder="Enter no. of lines"
                required
                min={1}
              />
              {error.includes("Lines") && (
                <span className="enq-field-error">{error}</span>
              )}
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                Winning Probability <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              <select
                name="Winprob"
                value={form.Winprob}
                onChange={handleChange}
                required
              >
                <option value="">-- Select --</option>
                <option value="LOW">LOW</option>
                <option value="MEDIUM">MEDIUM</option>
                <option value="HIGH">HIGH</option>
              </select>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
        {/* end enq-bottom-grid */}

        {/* ── ACTION BUTTONS ────────────────────────────────────────── */}
        <div className="enq-actions">
          <button type="reset" className="enq-btn-reset">
            Reset
          </button>
          <button type="submit" className="enq-btn-save" disabled={loading}>
            {loading ? "Saving..." : "Save"}
          </button>
        </div>
      </form>
    </div>
  );
}
 
==================== C:\Users\psarv\Desktop\q2psystemfrontend\src\pages\Enquiry\EditEnquiry.jsx ==================== 
import React, { useState, useEffect } from "react";
import axios from "axios";
import { useNavigate, useParams } from "react-router-dom";
import "./enquiry.css";

const API = import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL;

export default function EditEnquiry() {
  const { quotenumber } = useParams();
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const token = localStorage.getItem("token");
  const headers = { Authorization: `Bearer ${token}` };

  const [form, setForm] = useState(null);
  const [sno, setSno] = useState("");

  // Dropdown options
  const [customers, setCustomers] = useState([]);
  const [buyers, setBuyers] = useState([]);
  const [appEngineers, setAppEngineers] = useState([]);
  const [salesManagers, setSalesManagers] = useState([]);
  const [rfqTypes, setRfqTypes] = useState([]);
  const [rfqCategories, setRfqCategories] = useState([]);
  const [quoteStages, setQuoteStages] = useState([]);
  const [oppStages, setOppStages] = useState([]);
  const [endCountries, setEndCountries] = useState([]);
  const [industries, setIndustries] = useState([]);
  const [facingFactories, setFacingFactories] = useState([]);
  const [products, setProducts] = useState([]);

  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState("");

  // ── Format date to YYYY-MM-DD for <input type="date"> ──────────────────
  const toInputDate = (val) => {
    if (!val) return "";
    const d = new Date(val);
    if (isNaN(d)) return "";
    return d.toISOString().split("T")[0];
  };

  // ── Load dropdowns + existing record ───────────────────────────────────
  useEffect(() => {
    const get = (url) => axios.get(`${API}${url}`, { headers });

    Promise.all([
      get("/api/enquiry/getcustomers"),
      get("/api/enquiry/getappengineers"),
      get("/api/enquiry/getsalesmanagers"),
      get("/api/enquiry/getrfqt"),
      get("/api/enquiry/getqt"),
      get("/api/enquiry/getqs"),
      get("/api/enquiry/getendcountries"),
      get("/api/enquiry/getindustries"),
      get("/api/enquiry/getff"),
      get("/api/enquiry/getproducts"),
      get(`/api/enquiry/${encodeURIComponent(quotenumber)}`),
    ])
      .then(
        ([
          custRes,
          aeRes,
          salesRes,
          rfqtRes,
          qtRes,
          qsRes,
          ecRes,
          indRes,
          ffRes,
          prodRes,
          recordRes,
        ]) => {
          setCustomers(custRes.data);
          setAppEngineers(aeRes.data);
          setSalesManagers(salesRes.data);
          setRfqTypes(rfqtRes.data);
          setRfqCategories(qtRes.data);
          setQuoteStages(qsRes.data);
          setEndCountries(ecRes.data);
          setIndustries(indRes.data);
          setFacingFactories(ffRes.data);
          setProducts(prodRes.data);

          const r = recordRes.data;
          setSno(r.Sno);

          // Products stored as comma-separated string → array
          const productArr = r.Product
            ? r.Product.split(",")
                .map((p) => p.trim())
                .filter(Boolean)
            : [];

          setForm({
            Quotenumber: r.Quotenumber || "",
            Rev: r.Rev ?? 0,
            RFQREGDate: toInputDate(r.RFQREGDate),
            Salescontact: r.Salescontact || "",
            Deptuser: r.Deptuser || "",
            Customername: r.Customername || "",
            Customertype: r.Customertype || "",
            CustomerCountry: r.CustomerCountry || "",
            Buyername: r.Buyername || "",
            Groupname: r.Groupname || "",
            Currency: r.Currency || "",
            RFQType: r.RFQType || "",
            RFQTypeCustom: "",
            isCustomRFQType: false,
            Projectname: r.Projectname || "",
            Endusername: r.Endusername || "",
            EndCountry: r.EndCountry || "",
            EndIndustry: r.EndIndustry || "",
            EndIndustryCustom: "",
            isCustomEndIndustry: false,
            EndUse: "",
            RFQreference: r.RFQreference || "",
            RFQDate: toInputDate(r.RFQDate),
            RFQCategory: r.RFQCategory || "",
            Quotestage: r.Quotestage || "",
            Quotesubmitteddate: toInputDate(r.Quotesubmitteddate),
            Opportunitystage: r.Opportunitystage || "",
            Expectedorderdate: toInputDate(r.Expectedorderdate),
            EffEnqDate: toInputDate(r.EffEnqDate),
            enableEffEnqDate: !!r.EffEnqDate,
            CustomerdueDate: toInputDate(r.CustomerdueDate),
            ProposeddueDate: toInputDate(r.ProposeddueDate),
            Priority: r.Priority || "Low",
            Facingfactory: r.Facingfactory || "",
            FacingfactoryCustom: "",
            isCustomFacingfactory: false,
            Product: productArr,
            Totallineitems: r.Totallineitems || "",
            Winprob: r.Winprob || "",
            Comments: r.Comments || "",
            Reason: r.Reason || "",
            RevisedDate: toInputDate(r.RevisedDate),
            revision: r.Rev ?? 0,
          });

          setLoading(false);
        },
      )
      .catch(() => {
        setError("Failed to load enquiry data.");
        setLoading(false);
      });
  }, [quotenumber]);

  // ── Opportunity Stages based on Quote Stage ─────────────────────────────
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!form?.Quotestage) return;
    axios
      .get(`${API}/api/enquiry/getstatus?quotestage=${form.Quotestage}`, {
        headers,
      })
      .then((res) => setOppStages(res.data));
  }, [form?.Quotestage]);

  // ── Customer change → auto-fill type/country + buyers ──────────────────
  const handleCustomerChange = async (e) => {
    const cname = e.target.value;
    setForm((prev) => ({ ...prev, Customername: cname, Buyername: "" }));
    if (!cname) return;
    try {
      const [infoRes, buyerRes] = await Promise.all([
        axios.get(
          `${API}/api/enquiry/getcustomerinfo?customername=${encodeURIComponent(cname)}`,
          { headers },
        ),
        axios.get(
          `${API}/api/enquiry/getbuyers?customer=${encodeURIComponent(cname)}`,
          { headers },
        ),
      ]);
      setForm((prev) => ({
        ...prev,
        Customertype: infoRes.data.custtype || "",
        CustomerCountry: infoRes.data.country || "",
      }));
      setBuyers(buyerRes.data.map((b) => b[0]));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error(err);
    }
  };

  // Load buyers when form first loads (for existing customer)
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!form?.Customername) return;
    axios
      .get(
        `${API}/api/enquiry/getbuyers?customer=${encodeURIComponent(form.Customername)}`,
        { headers },
      )
      .then((res) => setBuyers(res.data.map((b) => b[0])));
  }, [form?.Customername]);

  // ── End Industry change → auto-fill EndUse ─────────────────────────────
  const handleIndustryChange = async (e) => {
    const val = e.target.value;
    setForm((prev) => ({ ...prev, EndIndustry: val }));
    if (!val) return;
    try {
      const res = await axios.get(
        `${API}/api/enquiry/getenduse?endind=${encodeURIComponent(val)}`,
        { headers },
      );
      setForm((prev) => ({ ...prev, EndUse: res.data.enduse || "" }));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error(err);
    }
  };

  // Load EndUse when form first loads (for existing industry)
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!form?.EndIndustry) return;
    axios
      .get(
        `${API}/api/enquiry/getenduse?endind=${encodeURIComponent(form.EndIndustry)}`,
        { headers },
      )
      .then((res) =>
        setForm((prev) => ({ ...prev, EndUse: res.data.enduse || "" })),
      );
  }, [form?.EndIndustry]);

  // ── Facing Factory change → filter products ────────────────────────────
  const handleFacingFactoryChange = async (val) => {
    setForm((prev) => ({ ...prev, Facingfactory: val, Product: [] }));
    if (!val) return;
    try {
      const res = await axios.get(
        `${API}/api/enquiry/getproducts?facingfactory=${encodeURIComponent(val)}`,
        { headers },
      );
      setProducts(res.data);
    } catch (err) {
      console.error(err);
    }
  };

  // ── Generic input handler ───────────────────────────────────────────────
  const handleChange = (e) => {
    const { name, value, type, checked } = e.target;
    setForm((prev) => ({
      ...prev,
      [name]: type === "checkbox" ? checked : value,
    }));
  };

  // ── Multi-select products ───────────────────────────────────────────────
  const handleProductChange = (e) => {
    const selected = Array.from(e.target.selectedOptions).map((o) => o.value);
    setForm((prev) => ({ ...prev, Product: selected }));
  };

  // ── Submit ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const handleSubmit = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setError("");

    if (parseInt(form.Totallineitems) < form.Product.length) {
      setError("Lines in RFQ must be ≥ number of products selected.");
      return;
    }

    const payload = {
      ...form,
      RFQType: form.isCustomRFQType ? form.RFQTypeCustom : form.RFQType,
      Facingfactory: form.isCustomFacingfactory
        ? form.FacingfactoryCustom
        : form.Facingfactory,
      EndIndustry: form.isCustomEndIndustry
        ? form.EndIndustryCustom
        : form.EndIndustry,
    };

    // Remove UI-only fields
    delete payload.RFQTypeCustom;
    delete payload.isCustomRFQType;
    delete payload.FacingfactoryCustom;
    delete payload.isCustomFacingfactory;
    delete payload.EndIndustryCustom;
    delete payload.isCustomEndIndustry;
    delete payload.EndUse;
    delete payload.enableEffEnqDate;

    setSaving(true);
    try {
      await axios.put(
        `${API}/api/enquiry/${encodeURIComponent(quotenumber)}`,
        payload,
        { headers },
      );
      alert("Enquiry updated successfully!");
      navigate("/enquiry");
    } catch (err) {
      setError(err.response?.data?.message || "Something went wrong.");
    } finally {
      setSaving(false);
    }
  };

  // ── Loading state ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  if (loading)
    return <div className="enq-loading">Loading enquiry data...</div>;
  if (!form) return <div className="enq-error">Enquiry not found.</div>;

  return (
    <div className="enq-wrapper">
      <div className="enq-header">
        <h3>
          Edit Enquiry
          <br />
          <span className="enq-sub">
            {form.Quotenumber} &nbsp;|&nbsp; Rev: {form.Rev}
          </span>
        </h3>
        <button className="enq-back-btn" onClick={() => navigate("/enquiry")}>
          ⌂ Back
        </button>
      </div>

      {error && <div className="enq-error">{error}</div>}

      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
        <div className="enq-main-grid">
          {/* ── CUSTOMER SECTION ──────────────────────────────────── */}
          <div className="enq-section">
            <div className="enq-section-title">Customer</div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                Customer Name <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              <select
                name="Customername"
                value={form.Customername}
                onChange={handleCustomerChange}
                required
              >
                <option value="">-- Select Customer --</option>
                {customers.map((c, i) => (
                  <option key={i} value={c[0]}>
                    {c[0]}
                  </option>
                ))}
              </select>
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>Customer Category</label>
              <p className="enq-readonly">{form.Customertype || "—"}</p>
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>Customer Country</label>
              <p className="enq-readonly">{form.CustomerCountry || "—"}</p>
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>Buyer Name</label>
              <select
                name="Buyername"
                value={form.Buyername}
                onChange={handleChange}
              >
                <option value="">-- Select Buyer --</option>
                {buyers.map((b, i) => (
                  <option key={i} value={b}>
                    {b}
                  </option>
                ))}
              </select>
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row enq-row-inline">
              <div>
                <label>Group</label>
                <p className="enq-readonly">{form.Groupname || "—"}</p>
              </div>
              <div>
                <label>
                  Currency <span className="req">*</span>
                </label>
                <select
                  name="Currency"
                  value={form.Currency}
                  onChange={handleChange}
                  required
                >
                  <option value="">-- Select --</option>
                  <option value="INR">INR</option>
                  <option value="USD">USD</option>
                  <option value="EUR">EUR</option>
                </select>
              </div>
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                End User Name <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              <input
                type="text"
                name="Endusername"
                value={form.Endusername}
                onChange={handleChange}
                maxLength={50}
                placeholder="Enter End User..."
                required
              />
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                End User Country <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              <select
                name="EndCountry"
                value={form.EndCountry}
                onChange={handleChange}
                required
              >
                <option value="">-- Select --</option>
                {endCountries.map((c, i) => (
                  <option key={i} value={c}>
                    {c}
                  </option>
                ))}
              </select>
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                End Industry <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              {form.isCustomEndIndustry ? (
                <div className="enq-custom-row">
                  <input
                    type="text"
                    name="EndIndustryCustom"
                    value={form.EndIndustryCustom}
                    onChange={handleChange}
                    placeholder="Enter End Industry..."
                    maxLength={45}
                  />
                  <input
                    type="checkbox"
                    checked={form.isCustomEndIndustry}
                    onChange={(e) =>
                      setForm((prev) => ({
                        ...prev,
                        isCustomEndIndustry: e.target.checked,
                      }))
                    }
                  />
                </div>
              ) : (
                <div className="enq-custom-row">
                  <select
                    name="EndIndustry"
                    value={form.EndIndustry}
                    onChange={handleIndustryChange}
                  >
                    <option value="">-- Select --</option>
                    {industries.map((ind, i) => (
                      <option key={i} value={ind}>
                        {ind}
                      </option>
                    ))}
                  </select>
                  <input
                    type="checkbox"
                    checked={form.isCustomEndIndustry}
                    onChange={(e) =>
                      setForm((prev) => ({
                        ...prev,
                        isCustomEndIndustry: e.target.checked,
                      }))
                    }
                  />
                </div>
              )}
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>End Use</label>
              <textarea name="EndUse" value={form.EndUse} rows={3} readOnly />
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* ── RFQ SECTION ───────────────────────────────────────── */}
          <div className="enq-section">
            <div className="enq-section-title">RFQ</div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                RFQ Receipt Date <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              <input
                type="date"
                name="RFQDate"
                value={form.RFQDate}
                onChange={handleChange}
                required
              />
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                App. Engineer <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              <select
                name="Deptuser"
                value={form.Deptuser}
                onChange={handleChange}
                required
              >
                <option value="">-- Select AE --</option>
                {appEngineers.map((ae, i) => (
                  <option key={i} value={ae}>
                    {ae}
                  </option>
                ))}
              </select>
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                Sales Contact <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              <select
                name="Salescontact"
                value={form.Salescontact}
                onChange={handleChange}
                required
              >
                <option value="">-- Select Sales --</option>
                {salesManagers.map((s, i) => (
                  <option key={i} value={s}>
                    {s}
                  </option>
                ))}
              </select>
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                Opportunity Type <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              {form.isCustomRFQType ? (
                <div className="enq-custom-row">
                  <input
                    type="text"
                    name="RFQTypeCustom"
                    value={form.RFQTypeCustom}
                    onChange={handleChange}
                    maxLength={45}
                    placeholder="Enter Opportunity Type..."
                  />
                  <input
                    type="checkbox"
                    checked={form.isCustomRFQType}
                    onChange={(e) =>
                      setForm((prev) => ({
                        ...prev,
                        isCustomRFQType: e.target.checked,
                      }))
                    }
                  />
                </div>
              ) : (
                <div className="enq-custom-row">
                  <select
                    name="RFQType"
                    value={form.RFQType}
                    onChange={handleChange}
                  >
                    <option value="">-- Select --</option>
                    {rfqTypes.map((r, i) => (
                      <option key={i} value={r}>
                        {r}
                      </option>
                    ))}
                  </select>
                  <input
                    type="checkbox"
                    checked={form.isCustomRFQType}
                    onChange={(e) =>
                      setForm((prev) => ({
                        ...prev,
                        isCustomRFQType: e.target.checked,
                      }))
                    }
                  />
                </div>
              )}
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                Category <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              <select
                name="RFQCategory"
                value={form.RFQCategory}
                onChange={handleChange}
                required
              >
                <option value="">-- Select --</option>
                {rfqCategories.map((c, i) => (
                  <option key={i} value={c}>
                    {c}
                  </option>
                ))}
              </select>
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                RFQ Reference <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              <textarea
                name="RFQreference"
                value={form.RFQreference}
                onChange={handleChange}
                rows={4}
                maxLength={250}
                placeholder="Enter RFQ Reference..."
                required
              />
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>Register Dt. Comments</label>
              <textarea
                name="Comments"
                value={form.Comments}
                onChange={handleChange}
                rows={4}
                maxLength={250}
                placeholder="Your Comments Here..."
              />
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
        {/* end enq-main-grid */}

        <hr className="enq-divider" />

        <div className="enq-bottom-grid">
          {/* ── QUOTE SECTION ─────────────────────────────────────── */}
          <div className="enq-section">
            <div className="enq-section-title">Quote</div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>Quote Number</label>
              <p className="enq-readonly enq-qn">{form.Quotenumber}</p>
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>Register Date</label>
              <input
                type="date"
                name="RFQREGDate"
                value={form.RFQREGDate}
                readOnly
              />
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                Stage <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              <select
                name="Quotestage"
                value={form.Quotestage}
                onChange={handleChange}
                required
              >
                <option value="">-- Select Stage --</option>
                {quoteStages.map((s, i) => (
                  <option key={i} value={s}>
                    {s}
                  </option>
                ))}
              </select>
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>Quote Submitted Date</label>
              <input
                type="date"
                name="Quotesubmitteddate"
                value={form.Quotesubmitteddate}
                onChange={handleChange}
                disabled={form.Quotestage?.toUpperCase() === "ENQUIRY"}
                className={
                  form.Quotestage?.toUpperCase() === "ENQUIRY"
                    ? "enq-disabled-field"
                    : ""
                }
              />
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                Opportunity Stage <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              <select
                name="Opportunitystage"
                value={form.Opportunitystage}
                onChange={handleChange}
                required
              >
                <option value="">-- Select --</option>
                {oppStages.map((s, i) => (
                  <option key={i} value={s}>
                    {s}
                  </option>
                ))}
              </select>
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>Revision</label>
              <p className="enq-readonly">{form.Rev}</p>
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                Expected Order Date <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              <input
                type="date"
                name="Expectedorderdate"
                value={form.Expectedorderdate}
                onChange={handleChange}
                required
              />
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row enq-row-inline">
              <div>
                <label>Effective Enquiry Date</label>
                <input
                  type="date"
                  name="EffEnqDate"
                  value={form.EffEnqDate}
                  onChange={handleChange}
                  disabled={!form.enableEffEnqDate}
                  className={!form.enableEffEnqDate ? "enq-disabled-field" : ""}
                />
              </div>
              <input
                type="checkbox"
                name="enableEffEnqDate"
                checked={form.enableEffEnqDate}
                onChange={handleChange}
                title="Enable Effective Enquiry Date"
              />
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>Priority</label>
              <select
                name="Priority"
                value={form.Priority}
                onChange={handleChange}
              >
                <option value="Low">Low</option>
                <option value="Medium">Medium</option>
                <option value="High">High</option>
              </select>
            </div>

            {/* Reason — shown only for Regret/Cancelled */}
            {["REGRET", "CANCELLED"].includes(
              form.Quotestage?.toUpperCase(),
            ) && (
              <div className="enq-row">
                <label>
                  Reason <span className="req">*</span>
                </label>
                <select
                  name="Reason"
                  value={form.Reason}
                  onChange={handleChange}
                  required
                >
                  <option value="">-- Select Reason --</option>
                  <option value="Price">Price</option>
                  <option value="Technical">Technical</option>
                  <option value="Delivery">Delivery</option>
                  <option value="Others">Others</option>
                </select>
              </div>
            )}

            {/* Revised Date — shown when Rev > 0 */}
            {form.Rev > 0 && (
              <div className="enq-row">
                <label>Revised Date</label>
                <input
                  type="date"
                  name="RevisedDate"
                  value={form.RevisedDate}
                  onChange={handleChange}
                />
              </div>
            )}
          </div>

          {/* ── PRODUCT SECTION ───────────────────────────────────── */}
          <div className="enq-section">
            <div className="enq-section-title">Product</div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                Facing Factory <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              {form.isCustomFacingfactory ? (
                <div className="enq-custom-row">
                  <input
                    type="text"
                    name="FacingfactoryCustom"
                    value={form.FacingfactoryCustom}
                    onChange={handleChange}
                    maxLength={25}
                    placeholder="Enter Facing Factory..."
                  />
                  <input
                    type="checkbox"
                    checked={form.isCustomFacingfactory}
                    onChange={(e) =>
                      setForm((prev) => ({
                        ...prev,
                        isCustomFacingfactory: e.target.checked,
                      }))
                    }
                  />
                </div>
              ) : (
                <div className="enq-custom-row">
                  <select
                    name="Facingfactory"
                    value={form.Facingfactory}
                    onChange={(e) => handleFacingFactoryChange(e.target.value)}
                  >
                    <option value="">-- Select --</option>
                    {facingFactories.map((f, i) => (
                      <option key={i} value={f}>
                        {f}
                      </option>
                    ))}
                  </select>
                  <input
                    type="checkbox"
                    checked={form.isCustomFacingfactory}
                    onChange={(e) =>
                      setForm((prev) => ({
                        ...prev,
                        isCustomFacingfactory: e.target.checked,
                      }))
                    }
                  />
                </div>
              )}
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                Product <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              <select
                name="Product"
                value={form.Product}
                onChange={handleProductChange}
                multiple
                required
              >
                {products.map((p, i) => (
                  <option key={i} value={p}>
                    {p}
                  </option>
                ))}
              </select>
              <small className="enq-hint">
                Hold Ctrl / Cmd to select multiple
              </small>
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                Project Name <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              <textarea
                name="Projectname"
                value={form.Projectname}
                onChange={handleChange}
                rows={4}
                maxLength={75}
                placeholder="Enter Project Name..."
                required
              />
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                Customer Due Date <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              <input
                type="date"
                name="CustomerdueDate"
                value={form.CustomerdueDate}
                onChange={handleChange}
                required
              />
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>Proposed Due Date</label>
              <input
                type="date"
                name="ProposeddueDate"
                value={form.ProposeddueDate}
                onChange={handleChange}
              />
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                Lines in RFQ <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              <input
                type="number"
                name="Totallineitems"
                value={form.Totallineitems}
                onChange={handleChange}
                maxLength={4}
                placeholder="Enter no. of lines"
                required
                min={1}
              />
            </div>

            <div className="enq-row">
              <label>
                Winning Probability <span className="req">*</span>
              </label>
              <select
                name="Winprob"
                value={form.Winprob}
                onChange={handleChange}
                required
              >
                <option value="">-- Select --</option>
                <option value="LOW">LOW</option>
                <option value="MEDIUM">MEDIUM</option>
                <option value="HIGH">HIGH</option>
              </select>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
        {/* end enq-bottom-grid */}

        {/* ── ACTION BUTTONS ──────────────────────────────────────── */}
        <div className="enq-actions">
          <button
            type="button"
            className="enq-btn-reset"
            onClick={() => navigate("/enquiry")}
          >
            Cancel
          </button>
          <button type="submit" className="enq-btn-save" disabled={saving}>
            {saving ? "Updating..." : "Update"}
          </button>
        </div>
      </form>
    </div>
  );
}

/* ── Filter Bar ───────────────────────────────────────── */

  display: flex; flex-wrap: wrap;

==================== C:\Users\psarv\Desktop\q2psystemfrontend\src\pages\Enquiry\EnquiryTable.jsx ==================== 
import React, { useState, useEffect, useMemo } from "react";
import axios from "axios";
import { useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
import "./enquiry.css";

const API = import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL;

const COLUMNS = [
  { key: "Quotenumber", label: "Quote No." },
  { key: "Rev", label: "Rev" },
  { key: "RFQREGDate", label: "Reg. Date" },
  { key: "Deptuser", label: "App. Engineer" },
  { key: "Salescontact", label: "Sales Contact" },
  { key: "Customername", label: "Customer" },
  { key: "Customertype", label: "Category" },
  { key: "CustomerCountry", label: "Cust. Country" },
  { key: "Buyername", label: "Buyer" },
  { key: "Groupname", label: "Group" },
  { key: "Currency", label: "Currency" },
  { key: "RFQType", label: "Opp. Type" },
  { key: "RFQDate", label: "RFQ Date" },
  { key: "RFQCategory", label: "Category" },
  { key: "RFQreference", label: "RFQ Ref." },
  { key: "Projectname", label: "Project" },
  { key: "Endusername", label: "End User" },
  { key: "EndCountry", label: "End Country" },
  { key: "EndIndustry", label: "End Industry" },
  { key: "Facingfactory", label: "Facing Factory" },
  { key: "Product", label: "Product" },
  { key: "Quotestage", label: "Stage" },
  { key: "Opportunitystage", label: "Opp. Stage" },
  { key: "Quotesubmitteddate", label: "Submitted Date" },
  { key: "Totallineitems", label: "Lines" },
  { key: "Winprob", label: "Win Prob." },
  { key: "Expectedorderdate", label: "Exp. Order Date" },
  { key: "CustomerdueDate", label: "Cust. Due Date" },
  { key: "ProposeddueDate", label: "Prop. Due Date" },
  { key: "EffEnqDate", label: "Eff. Enq. Date" },
  { key: "Priority", label: "Priority" },
  { key: "Comments", label: "Comments" },
];

const STAGE_COLORS = {
  Enquiry: "#e3f2fd",
  "Technical Offer": "#fff8e1",
  "Priced Offer": "#f3e5f5",
  "Price Book Order": "#e8f5e9",
  Regret: "#ffebee",
  Cancelled: "#f5f5f5",
};

function formatDate(val) {
  if (!val) return "—";
  const d = new Date(val);
  if (isNaN(d)) return val;
  return d.toLocaleDateString("en-GB"); // dd/mm/yyyy
}

export default function EnquiryTable() {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const token = localStorage.getItem("token");
  const headers = { Authorization: `Bearer ${token}` };

  const [rows, setRows] = useState([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState("");

  // ── Filters ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const [search, setSearch] = useState("");
  const [filterStage, setFilterStage] = useState("");
  const [filterAE, setFilterAE] = useState("");
  const [filterSales, setFilterSales] = useState("");
  const [filterPriority, setFilterPriority] = useState("");
  const [filterYear, setFilterYear] = useState("");

  // ── Sort ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const [sortKey, setSortKey] = useState("Sno");
  const [sortDir, setSortDir] = useState("desc");

  // ── Pagination ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const [page, setPage] = useState(1);
  const PAGE_SIZE = 20;

  // ── Load data ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  useEffect(() => {
    setLoading(true);
    axios
      .get(`${API}/api/enquiry/`, { headers })
      .then((res) => {
        setRows(res.data);
        setLoading(false);
      })
      .catch(() => {
        setError("Failed to load enquiries.");
        setLoading(false);
      });
  }, []);

  // ── Unique filter options ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const stages = useMemo(
    () => [...new Set(rows.map((r) => r.Quotestage).filter(Boolean))],
    [rows],
  );
  const aeList = useMemo(
    () => [...new Set(rows.map((r) => r.Deptuser).filter(Boolean))].sort(),
    [rows],
  );
  const salesList = useMemo(
    () => [...new Set(rows.map((r) => r.Salescontact).filter(Boolean))].sort(),
    [rows],
  );
  const years = useMemo(
    () =>
      [...new Set(rows.map((r) => r.RFQREGDate?.slice(0, 4)).filter(Boolean))]
        .sort()
        .reverse(),
    [rows],
  );

  // ── Filtered + sorted data ────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const filtered = useMemo(() => {
    let data = [...rows];

    if (search) {
      const q = search.toLowerCase();
      data = data.filter((r) =>
        COLUMNS.some((col) =>
          String(r[col.key] ?? "")
            .toLowerCase()
            .includes(q),
        ),
      );
    }
    if (filterStage) data = data.filter((r) => r.Quotestage === filterStage);
    if (filterAE) data = data.filter((r) => r.Deptuser === filterAE);
    if (filterSales) data = data.filter((r) => r.Salescontact === filterSales);
    if (filterPriority)
      data = data.filter((r) => r.Priority === filterPriority);
    if (filterYear)
      data = data.filter((r) => r.RFQREGDate?.startsWith(filterYear));

    data.sort((a, b) => {
      const va = a[sortKey] ?? "";
      const vb = b[sortKey] ?? "";
      if (va < vb) return sortDir === "asc" ? -1 : 1;
      if (va > vb) return sortDir === "asc" ? 1 : -1;
      return 0;
    });

    return data;
  }, [
    rows,
    search,
    filterStage,
    filterAE,
    filterSales,
    filterPriority,
    filterYear,
    sortKey,
    sortDir,
  ]);

  const totalPages = Math.ceil(filtered.length / PAGE_SIZE);
  const paginated = filtered.slice((page - 1) * PAGE_SIZE, page * PAGE_SIZE);

  const handleSort = (key) => {
    if (sortKey === key) setSortDir((d) => (d === "asc" ? "desc" : "asc"));
    else {
      setSortKey(key);
      setSortDir("asc");
    }
    setPage(1);
  };

  const resetFilters = () => {
    setSearch("");
    setFilterStage("");
    setFilterAE("");
    setFilterSales("");
    setFilterPriority("");
    setFilterYear("");
    setPage(1);
  };

  // ── Stage badge color ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const stageBg = (stage) => STAGE_COLORS[stage] || "#f9f9f9";

  return (
    <div className="enq-wrapper">
      {/* ── Header ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */}
      <div className="enq-header">
        <h3>
          Enquiry Register
          <br />
          <span className="enq-sub">Total: {filtered.length} records</span>
        </h3>
        <button
          className="enq-btn-save"
          onClick={() => navigate("/enquiry/add")}
        >
          + New Enquiry
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* ── Filter Bar ──────────────────────────────────────────────────── */}
      <div className="enq-filter-bar">
        <input
          className="enq-search"
          placeholder="🔍  Search all fields..."
          value={search}
          onChange={(e) => {
            setSearch(e.target.value);
            setPage(1);
          }}
        />

        <select
          value={filterYear}
          onChange={(e) => {
            setFilterYear(e.target.value);
            setPage(1);
          }}
        >
          <option value="">All Years</option>
          {years.map((y) => (
            <option key={y} value={y}>
              {y}
            </option>
          ))}
        </select>

        <select
          value={filterStage}
          onChange={(e) => {
            setFilterStage(e.target.value);
            setPage(1);
          }}
        >
          <option value="">All Stages</option>
          {stages.map((s) => (
            <option key={s} value={s}>
              {s}
            </option>
          ))}
        </select>

        <select
          value={filterAE}
          onChange={(e) => {
            setFilterAE(e.target.value);
            setPage(1);
          }}
        >
          <option value="">All AE</option>
          {aeList.map((a) => (
            <option key={a} value={a}>
              {a}
            </option>
          ))}
        </select>

        <select
          value={filterSales}
          onChange={(e) => {
            setFilterSales(e.target.value);
            setPage(1);
          }}
        >
          <option value="">All Sales</option>
          {salesList.map((s) => (
            <option key={s} value={s}>
              {s}
            </option>
          ))}
        </select>

        <select
          value={filterPriority}
          onChange={(e) => {
            setFilterPriority(e.target.value);
            setPage(1);
          }}
        >
          <option value="">All Priority</option>
          <option value="Low">Low</option>
          <option value="Medium">Medium</option>
          <option value="High">High</option>
        </select>

        <button className="enq-btn-reset" onClick={resetFilters}>
          Clear
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* ── Error / Loading ──────────────────────────────────────────────── */}
      {error && <div className="enq-error">{error}</div>}
      {loading && <div className="enq-loading">Loading enquiries...</div>}

      {/* ── Table ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */}
      {!loading && (
        <div className="enq-table-scroll">
          <table className="enq-table">
            <thead>
              <tr>
                <th className="enq-th-action">Action</th>
                {COLUMNS.map((col) => (
                  <th
                    key={col.key}
                    onClick={() => handleSort(col.key)}
                    className="enq-th-sortable"
                    title={`Sort by ${col.label}`}
                  >
                    {col.label}
                    {sortKey === col.key
                      ? sortDir === "asc"
                        ? " ▲"
                        : " ▼"
                      : " ⇅"}
                  </th>
                ))}
              </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
              {paginated.length === 0 ? (
                <tr>
                  <td colSpan={COLUMNS.length + 1} className="enq-no-data">
                    No records found.
                  </td>
                </tr>
              ) : (
                paginated.map((row) => (
                  <tr
                    key={`${row.Quotenumber}-${row.Rev}`}
                    style={{ backgroundColor: stageBg(row.Quotestage) }}
                  >
                    <td className="enq-td-action">
                      <button
                        className="enq-edit-btn"
                        title="Edit Enquiry"
                        onClick={() =>
                          navigate(`/enquiry/edit/${row.Quotenumber}`)
                        }
                      >
                        ✏️
                      </button>
                    </td>

                    {COLUMNS.map((col) => {
                      const val = row[col.key];
                      const isDate = col.key.toLowerCase().includes("date");
                      const isStage = col.key === "Quotestage";
                      const isPriority = col.key === "Priority";

                      return (
                        <td key={col.key} className="enq-td">
                          {isDate ? (
                            formatDate(val)
                          ) : isStage ? (
                            <span
                              className="enq-stage-badge"
                              style={{ background: stageBg(val) }}
                            >
                              {val || "—"}
                            </span>
                          ) : isPriority ? (
                            <span
                              className={`enq-priority-badge enq-priority-${(val || "low").toLowerCase()}`}
                            >
                              {val || "—"}
                            </span>
                          ) : (
                            (val ?? "—")
                          )}
                        </td>
                      );
                    })}
                  </tr>
                ))
              )}
            </tbody>
          </table>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* ── Pagination ──────────────────────────────────────────────────── */}
      {!loading && totalPages > 1 && (
        <div className="enq-pagination">
          <button
            disabled={page === 1}
            onClick={() => setPage((p) => p - 1)}
            className="enq-page-btn"
          >
            ‹ Prev
          </button>

          {Array.from({ length: totalPages }, (_, i) => i + 1)
            .filter(
              (p) => p === 1 || p === totalPages || Math.abs(p - page) <= 2,
            )
            .reduce((acc, p, idx, arr) => {
              if (idx > 0 && p - arr[idx - 1] > 1)
                acc.push(
                  <span key={`ellipsis-${p}`} className="enq-ellipsis">
                    …
                  </span>,
                );
              acc.push(
                <button
                  key={p}
                  onClick={() => setPage(p)}
                  className={`enq-page-btn ${p === page ? "enq-page-active" : ""}`}
                >
                  {p}
                </button>,
              );
              return acc;
            }, [])}

          <button
            disabled={page === totalPages}
            onClick={() => setPage((p) => p + 1)}
            className="enq-page-btn"
          >
            Next ›
          </button>

          <span className="enq-page-info">
            Page {page} of {totalPages} &nbsp;|&nbsp; {filtered.length} records
          </span>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
 
==================== C:\Users\psarv\Desktop\q2psystemfrontend\src\pages\masters\Buyer.jsx ==================== 
import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from "react";
import { useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
import axios from "axios";
import DashboardNavbar from "../../components/DashboardNavbar";
import { getAuth, isLoggedIn } from "../../utils/auth";

const API = "http://localhost:5001/api/buyer";
const PAGE_SIZE = 50;

const emptyForm = {
  Customer: "",
  Buyername: "",
  Designation: "",
  email1: "",
  email2: "",
  contact1: "",
  contact2: "",
  contact3: "",
  Location: "",
  Segment: "",
  Comments: "",
};

export default function Buyer() {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const { token, user } = getAuth();
  const role = user?.role;
  const canEdit = role === "Admin" || role === "Manager";

  const [allData, setAllData] = useState([]);
  const [filtered, setFiltered] = useState([]);
  const [page, setPage] = useState(1);
  const [searchVal, setSearchVal] = useState("");

  const [panel, setPanel] = useState(null);
  const [form, setForm] = useState(emptyForm);
  const [editSno, setEditSno] = useState(null);
  const [fieldErrors, setFieldErrors] = useState({});
  const [alert, setAlert] = useState({ msg: "", type: "" });
  const [confirmModal, setConfirmModal] = useState({
    show: false,
    sno: null,
    currentStatus: "",
  });
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [customers, setCustomers] = useState([]);

  const headers = { Authorization: `Bearer ${token}` };

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!isLoggedIn()) navigate("/login", { replace: true });
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    axios
      .get(`${API}/customers`, { headers })
      .then((r) => setCustomers(r.data))
      .catch(() => {});
  }, [token]);

  const showAlert = (msg, type) => {
    setAlert({ msg, type });
    setTimeout(() => setAlert({ msg: "", type: "" }), 3500);
  };

  const fetchData = useCallback(async () => {
    try {
      const { data } = await axios.get(API, { headers });
      setAllData(data);
      setFiltered(data);
      setPage(1);
    } catch {
      showAlert("Failed to load data.", "danger");
    }
  }, [token]);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchData();
  }, [fetchData]);

  // ── Auto-fill Location & Segment on customer select ───────────────────────
  const handleCustomerChange = (custname) => {
    const found = customers.find((c) => c.customername === custname);
    if (found) {
      const segment =
        (found.customercountry || "").toUpperCase() === "INDIA"
          ? "Domestic"
          : "Export";
      setForm((prev) => ({
        ...prev,
        Customer: custname,
        Location: found.Location,
        Segment: segment,
      }));
    } else {
      setForm((prev) => ({
        ...prev,
        Customer: custname,
        Location: "",
        Segment: "",
      }));
    }
  };

  // ── Live Search across ALL columns ────────────────────────────────────────
  const handleLiveSearch = (e) => {
    const val = e.target.value;
    setSearchVal(val);
    const q = val.trim().toLowerCase();
    setFiltered(
      !q
        ? allData
        : allData.filter((row) =>
            [
              row.Customer,
              row.Buyername,
              row.Designation,
              row.email1,
              row.email2,
              row.contact,
              row.Location,
              row.Segment,
              row.Comments,
              row.status,
            ]
              .map((v) => (v || "").toLowerCase())
              .some((v) => v.includes(q)),
          ),
    );
    setPage(1);
  };

  const handleClear = () => {
    setSearchVal("");
    setFiltered(allData);
    setPage(1);
  };

  // ── Pagination ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const totalPages = Math.ceil(filtered.length / PAGE_SIZE);
  const paginated = filtered.slice((page - 1) * PAGE_SIZE, page * PAGE_SIZE);

  // ── Panel ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const openAdd = () => {
    setForm(emptyForm);
    setFieldErrors({});
    setAlert({ msg: "", type: "" });
    setPanel("add");
  };

  const openEdit = (row) => {
    if (row.status === "Inactive") {
      showAlert(
        `"${row.Buyername}" is Inactive and cannot be edited.`,
        "warning",
      );
      return;
    }
    const contacts = (row.contact || "").split(",");
    setForm({
      Customer: row.Customer || "",
      Buyername: row.Buyername || "",
      Designation: row.Designation || "",
      email1: row.email1 || "",
      email2: row.email2 || "",
      contact1: contacts[0]?.trim() || "",
      contact2: contacts[1]?.trim() || "",
      contact3: contacts[2]?.trim() || "",
      Location: row.Location || "",
      Segment: row.Segment || "",
      Comments: row.Comments || "",
    });
    setEditSno(row.Sno);
    setFieldErrors({});
    setAlert({ msg: "", type: "" });
    setPanel("edit");
  };

  const closePanel = () => {
    setPanel(null);
    setForm(emptyForm);
    setFieldErrors({});
  };

  // ── Duplicate checks ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const checkField = async (params) => {
    try {
      const query = new URLSearchParams(params).toString();
      const { data } = await axios.get(`${API}/check?${query}`, { headers });
      if (data.exists)
        setFieldErrors((prev) => ({ ...prev, [data.field]: data.message }));
      else {
        const key = Object.keys(params)[0];
        setFieldErrors((prev) => {
          const e = { ...prev };
          delete e[key];
          return e;
        });
      }
    } catch {}
  };

  const clearErr = (field) =>
    setFieldErrors((prev) => {
      const e = { ...prev };
      delete e[field];
      return e;
    });

  // ── ADD ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const handleAdd = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    if (Object.keys(fieldErrors).length > 0) return;
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const { data } = await axios.post(API, form, { headers });
      showAlert(data.message, "success");
      closePanel();
      fetchData();
    } catch (err) {
      showAlert(err.response?.data?.message || "Error adding buyer.", "danger");
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  // ── EDIT ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const handleEdit = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const {
        Designation,
        email1,
        email2,
        contact1,
        contact2,
        contact3,
        Comments,
      } = form;
      const { data } = await axios.put(
        `${API}/${editSno}`,
        { Designation, email1, email2, contact1, contact2, contact3, Comments },
        { headers },
      );
      showAlert(data.message, "success");
      closePanel();
      fetchData();
    } catch (err) {
      showAlert(
        err.response?.data?.message || "Error updating buyer.",
        "danger",
      );
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  // ── TOGGLE ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const handleToggle = async () => {
    const { sno, currentStatus } = confirmModal;
    const newStatus = currentStatus === "Active" ? "Inactive" : "Active";
    setConfirmModal({ show: false, sno: null, currentStatus: "" });
    try {
      await axios.patch(
        `${API}/toggle/${sno}`,
        { status: newStatus },
        { headers },
      );
      fetchData();
    } catch {
      showAlert("Failed to toggle status.", "danger");
    }
  };

  const lockedStyle = { backgroundColor: "#e9ecef" };

  return (
    <>
      <DashboardNavbar />
      <div className="container-fluid px-3 py-3">
        {/* Breadcrumb */}
        <div className="d-flex align-items-center gap-2 mb-3">
          <button
            className="btn btn-sm back-btn"
            onClick={() => navigate("/masters")}
          >
            <i className="bi bi-arrow-left-circle-fill me-1"></i>Back
          </button>
          <span className="text-muted" style={{ fontSize: "0.88rem" }}>
            Masters &rsaquo; <strong>Buyer</strong>
          </span>
        </div>

        <h5 className="master-page-title mb-3">
          <i className="bi bi-people-fill me-2"></i>Buyer Master
        </h5>

        {alert.msg && (
          <div className={`alert alert-${alert.type} py-2`} role="alert">
            {alert.msg}
          </div>
        )}

        {/* ── Live Search Toolbar ───────────────────────────────── */}
        <div className="master-toolbar mb-3 d-flex flex-wrap align-items-center gap-2">
          <div>
            <label className="form-label mb-1" style={{ fontSize: "0.8rem" }}>
              Search (All Columns)
            </label>
            <input
              type="text"
              className="form-control form-control-sm"
              style={{ width: "300px" }}
              placeholder="Search Customer, Buyer, Email, Contact, Segment..."
              value={searchVal}
              onChange={handleLiveSearch}
            />
          </div>
          {searchVal && (
            <button
              className="btn btn-sm btn-outline-secondary align-self-end"
              onClick={handleClear}
            >
              <i className="bi bi-x-circle me-1"></i>Clear
            </button>
          )}
          <div className="ms-auto d-flex align-items-center gap-2">
            <span className="text-muted" style={{ fontSize: "0.82rem" }}>
              Records: <strong>{filtered.length}</strong>
            </span>
            {canEdit && (
              <button
                className="btn btn-sm btn-primary-custom"
                onClick={openAdd}
              >
                <i className="bi bi-plus-circle-fill me-1"></i>Add
              </button>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* ── Table + Panel ────────────────────────────────────────── */}
        <div className="d-flex gap-3" style={{ minHeight: "60vh" }}>
          {/* Table */}
          <div
            className="master-table-wrapper"
            style={{
              flex: panel ? "0 0 55%" : "1",
              transition: "flex 0.3s",
              overflowX: "auto",
            }}
          >
            <table className="table table-bordered table-hover master-table mb-0">
              <thead>
                <tr>
                  <th style={{ width: "4%" }}>S.No</th>
                  <th style={{ width: "20%" }}>Customer</th>
                  <th style={{ width: "16%" }}>Buyer Name</th>
                  <th style={{ width: "14%" }}>Designation</th>
                  <th style={{ width: "18%" }}>Email 1</th>
                  <th style={{ width: "14%" }}>Contact</th>
                  <th style={{ width: "8%" }}>Segment</th>
                  <th style={{ width: "6%" }}>Action</th>
                </tr>
              </thead>
              <tbody>
                {paginated.length === 0 ? (
                  <tr>
                    <td colSpan={8} className="text-center text-muted py-4">
                      No records found.
                    </td>
                  </tr>
                ) : (
                  paginated.map((row, idx) => (
                    <tr
                      key={row.Sno}
                      onDoubleClick={() => canEdit && openEdit(row)}
                      style={{ cursor: canEdit ? "pointer" : "default" }}
                      className={
                        panel === "edit" && editSno === row.Sno
                          ? "table-active"
                          : ""
                      }
                    >
                      <td>{(page - 1) * PAGE_SIZE + idx + 1}</td>
                      <td>{row.Customer}</td>
                      <td>{row.Buyername}</td>
                      <td>{row.Designation || "—"}</td>
                      <td style={{ fontSize: "0.82rem" }}>
                        {row.email1 || "—"}
                      </td>
                      <td style={{ fontSize: "0.82rem" }}>
                        {row.contact || "—"}
                      </td>
                      <td>
                        <span
                          className={`badge ${
                            row.Segment === "Domestic"
                              ? "bg-info text-dark"
                              : "bg-warning text-dark"
                          }`}
                        >
                          {row.Segment || "—"}
                        </span>
                      </td>
                      <td className="text-center">
                        {canEdit ? (
                          <button
                            className={`btn btn-xs status-btn ${
                              row.status === "Active"
                                ? "status-active"
                                : "status-inactive"
                            }`}
                            onClick={() =>
                              setConfirmModal({
                                show: true,
                                sno: row.Sno,
                                currentStatus: row.status,
                              })
                            }
                          >
                            {row.status}
                          </button>
                        ) : (
                          <span
                            className={`badge ${row.status === "Active" ? "bg-success" : "bg-secondary"}`}
                          >
                            {row.status}
                          </span>
                        )}
                      </td>
                    </tr>
                  ))
                )}
              </tbody>
            </table>

            {/* Pagination */}
            {totalPages > 1 && (
              <div className="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center mt-2 px-1">
                <small className="text-muted">
                  Page {page} of {totalPages}
                </small>
                <div className="d-flex gap-1">
                  <button
                    className="btn btn-sm btn-outline-secondary"
                    disabled={page === 1}
                    onClick={() => setPage((p) => p - 1)}
                  >
                    <i className="bi bi-chevron-left"></i>
                  </button>
                  {Array.from({ length: totalPages }, (_, i) => i + 1)
                    .filter(
                      (p) =>
                        p === 1 || p === totalPages || Math.abs(p - page) <= 2,
                    )
                    .map((p, i, arr) => (
                      <>
                        {i > 0 && arr[i - 1] !== p - 1 && (
                          <span key={`e${p}`} className="btn btn-sm disabled">
                            …
                          </span>
                        )}
                        <button
                          key={p}
                          className={`btn btn-sm ${page === p ? "btn-primary-custom" : "btn-outline-secondary"}`}
                          onClick={() => setPage(p)}
                        >
                          {p}
                        </button>
                      </>
                    ))}
                  <button
                    className="btn btn-sm btn-outline-secondary"
                    disabled={page === totalPages}
                    onClick={() => setPage((p) => p + 1)}
                  >
                    <i className="bi bi-chevron-right"></i>
                  </button>
                </div>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>

          {/* ── Side Panel ─────────────────────────────────────── */}
          {panel && (
            <div
              className="master-side-panel"
              style={{ flex: "0 0 43%", maxHeight: "82vh", overflowY: "auto" }}
            >
              <div className="panel-header d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center mb-3">
                <h6
                  className="mb-0"
                  style={{ color: "#800000", fontWeight: 700 }}
                >
                  <i
                    className={`bi ${panel === "add" ? "bi-plus-circle-fill" : "bi-pencil-fill"} me-2`}
                  ></i>
                  {panel === "add" ? "Create Buyer" : "Modify Buyer"}
                </h6>
                <button
                  className="btn btn-sm btn-outline-secondary"
                  onClick={closePanel}
                >
                  <i className="bi bi-x-lg"></i>
                </button>
              </div>

              <form
                onSubmit={panel === "add" ? handleAdd : handleEdit}
                noValidate
              >
                {/* Customer */}
                <div className="mb-2">
                  <label className="form-label panel-label">
                    Customer <span className="text-danger">*</span>
                  </label>
                  {panel === "add" ? (
                    <select
                      className="form-select form-select-sm"
                      value={form.Customer}
                      onChange={(e) => {
                        handleCustomerChange(e.target.value);
                        clearErr("buyer");
                      }}
                      required
                    >
                      <option value="">-- Select Customer --</option>
                      {customers.map((c, i) => (
                        <option key={i} value={c.customername}>
                          {c.customername}
                          {c.Location ? ` — ${c.Location}` : ""}
                        </option>
                      ))}
                    </select>
                  ) : (
                    <input
                      type="text"
                      className="form-control form-control-sm"
                      value={form.Customer}
                      readOnly
                      style={lockedStyle}
                    />
                  )}
                </div>

                {/* Location — locked always */}
                <div className="mb-2">
                  <label className="form-label panel-label">Location</label>
                  <input
                    type="text"
                    className="form-control form-control-sm"
                    value={form.Location}
                    readOnly
                    style={lockedStyle}
                    placeholder="Auto-filled from Customer"
                  />
                </div>

                {/* Buyer Name — locked in edit */}
                <div className="mb-2">
                  <label className="form-label panel-label">
                    Buyer Name <span className="text-danger">*</span>
                  </label>
                  <input
                    type="text"
                    className={`form-control form-control-sm ${fieldErrors.buyer ? "is-invalid" : ""}`}
                    value={form.Buyername}
                    onChange={(e) => {
                      setForm({ ...form, Buyername: e.target.value });
                      clearErr("buyer");
                    }}
                    onBlur={() =>
                      panel === "add" &&
                      form.Customer &&
                      form.Buyername &&
                      checkField({
                        customer: form.Customer,
                        buyer: form.Buyername,
                      })
                    }
                    readOnly={panel === "edit"}
                    style={panel === "edit" ? lockedStyle : {}}
                    required={panel === "add"}
                    maxLength={30}
                    placeholder="Enter Buyer Name"
                  />
                  {fieldErrors.buyer && (
                    <div className="invalid-feedback">{fieldErrors.buyer}</div>
                  )}
                </div>

                {/* Designation */}
                <div className="mb-2">
                  <label className="form-label panel-label">Designation</label>
                  <input
                    type="text"
                    className="form-control form-control-sm"
                    value={form.Designation}
                    onChange={(e) =>
                      setForm({ ...form, Designation: e.target.value })
                    }
                    maxLength={45}
                    placeholder="e.g. Purchase Manager"
                  />
                </div>

                {/* Email 1 */}
                <div className="mb-2">
                  <label className="form-label panel-label">Email 1</label>
                  <input
                    type="email"
                    className={`form-control form-control-sm ${fieldErrors.email1 ? "is-invalid" : ""}`}
                    value={form.email1}
                    onChange={(e) => {
                      setForm({ ...form, email1: e.target.value });
                      clearErr("email1");
                    }}
                    onBlur={() =>
                      form.email1 && checkField({ email1: form.email1 })
                    }
                    maxLength={45}
                    placeholder="abc@gmail.com"
                  />
                  {fieldErrors.email1 && (
                    <div className="invalid-feedback">{fieldErrors.email1}</div>
                  )}
                </div>

                {/* Email 2 */}
                <div className="mb-2">
                  <label className="form-label panel-label">Email 2</label>
                  <input
                    type="email"
                    className={`form-control form-control-sm ${fieldErrors.email2 ? "is-invalid" : ""}`}
                    value={form.email2}
                    onChange={(e) => {
                      setForm({ ...form, email2: e.target.value });
                      clearErr("email2");
                    }}
                    onBlur={() =>
                      form.email2 && checkField({ email2: form.email2 })
                    }
                    maxLength={45}
                    placeholder="abc@gmail.com"
                  />
                  {fieldErrors.email2 && (
                    <div className="invalid-feedback">{fieldErrors.email2}</div>
                  )}
                </div>

                {/* Mobile */}
                <div className="mb-2">
                  <label className="form-label panel-label">Mobile</label>
                  <input
                    type="text"
                    className={`form-control form-control-sm ${fieldErrors.contact1 ? "is-invalid" : ""}`}
                    value={form.contact1}
